sbyar /
par khams dang mtsho kha phyogs su 'brum nag yod tshul byung bar ded rang gis nad bdag stobs 'joms dang brag sna chos rjes gtsos pa'i gra tshang gi gra pa kha shas kyis lha sa nas 'dod khams dbang phyug ma'i bzlog pa dang 'brel ba'i zor 'phangs pas nad mtshams chod pa'i 'phrod lam tsha bar byung /
des mtshon snga phyi du mar stod smad tshor mchod bar nye ba'i 'brum rims la 'di gnas btang ba dang phyogs so so'i sngags 'chang rnams byed du btsud pa'i mdos zor kha bsgyur tshes phan thogs tsam byung bar mngon /
gter sgrom nas chu tshan blangs ba'i zhag bdun gyi bar 'phrod bsten byas te nyi shu'i nyin rgya nag gi mi sna tshor skyer sgang lugs kyi thugs rje chen po /

rgya nag tu glang po che gson po'ang mang du mthong chung mche ba de 'dra yod pa de mi 'dug pas khyad du 'phags pa zhig yin par mngon /

gos chen dngul gyi tha phag gi rten lan dang bcas bskur /
a pa la'i skor bcas drag rigs sum cu lhag la nang rten rags rim gyi mjal ka /

rje btsun rin po che grags pa dang dpal chen 'od po'i dbu thod dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis gdan sa gong nas gden drangs te rtses dang bsam gtan gling du bzhugs pa sna'u sdong rtse brgyud rin spungs pa'i nang rten gtsigs can chos mdzad rgyal bo don grub kyis lho brag tu khyer ba tsha mo btsun ma zhig gi lag nas byung /

rmi ru bla ma brag sgor ba 'byams pa'i padma bka' thang gi rtsod yig la ka tshal zur ba rigs 'dzin dkon mchog lhun grub kyis dri lan mdzad pa ston pa dang 'brum pa las grol ba'i legs so brjod pa'i snyan tshig dar bcas bsrings byung ba khor bshes rab dang yon tan gnyis ka che gshis tshig skyon rnon po de la bltos pa'i lan 'debs lod pa rang ma byung 'dug pas legs so'i 'phrin yig snyan ngag gi lam nas drangs /
de yang gser mdog can pa'i dge bshes rgya ma brtsod btun rong pa'i rab 'byams pas thang yig la dgag pha btang ba'i dum bu zhig sngar mthong myong ba lo chigs snga phyi sogs 'gal 'du brdabs pa dang rtog ge ba'i rigs pa nas drangs pa'i tshig skyen shin tu snang ba dngos lan 'debs bya 'debs byed dang bral bar snang /

dngos lan btab kyang bzhengs pas che ru mi 'gyo /

mdo mdzangs blun du byang chub sems dpa' da ste zhag bdun nas lus la mar me stong 'dzugs pas lta ba la shog ces zla lam gyi bar pho nya bkye ba 'dug pa sprul pa las tha mal ba'i rgyas mi khebs pa'i rgyu mtshan zhag bdun thog tu lus la mar me 'dzugs par zla lam gyi sa nas lta mkhan rnams mi 'byor ba lta bu'i tshig skyon tsam 'khungs ci yod /

'khrungs rabs so bzhi pa'i lung rgyun la sa dge bka' brgyud mtha' dag tshad mar 'dzin yang slob dpon gyis bstan bcos mdzad 'phral rten 'brel gyi dbang las stag gi sku lus zos pa sus kyang mtshor ba ring zhig nas dpe rnyed pa'i le'u so bzhi yan ma gtogs de phyin chad char chus zos te ma byung ba'i gtam khungs mar grags pas dpa' bos lung su la gnang /

sku /
'ched ka spyan snga gsum dang phrad /

ma 'ongs pa na 'di 'dra'i rigs kyis zhal gzigs dang mngon mkhyen sogs kyi sgro btags a tsi bar mi 'gro ba'i nges pa med na'ang de 'dra yong re'i ltogs lam ni kyang rang ngos byang chub sgrub pa'i 'phrin las zhu ba'i ched gra slob nyi shus zhal la gtor chog pho nya myur mgyogs bskang gso lhan thabs dang bcas pa zla ba bcu pa'i nyer lnga nas 'tshubs pa'i nyin lnga /

lha sa byang gling pas mchod yon la bsnyen bkur gyi skal ba'i dkar spro dmar spro'i gzhis len ster cha sogs sbams mtho ba pa teg /
sbus srang gser khang pas dkar spro'i spom 'bul bstar /
chos 'khor yang rtse'i gra pa blo bzang tshe ring gis gsar rtsom phar phyin gyi rgyugs sprad /
nyer brgyad la par pa tshor rta mgrin skyer sgang lugs /
gru nas bshad pa'i 'byung 'dul /
chAn su'i gyi mi sna nyung bsdus la tshe dbang grub rgyal ma /
'jam dbyangs a rab tsa na gtso rkyang /
thugs rje chen po gtso 'khor gsum pa /
rdzing phyi mkhan po co ne chos rje /
rab brtan hung tha'i ji'i dge tshul no gon d+ha ra /
kong po dar khan em chi /
se chen rgyal po sogs kyi mi sna khag rnams la skyer sgang lugs kyi thugs rje chen po /
'byung 'dul gyi rjes gnang rnams bskur /
se chen rgyal po'i mi sna no yon dbon po /
yun gling par zhus pa gsum sogs dge slong bcu gsum /
thar rgyas chos mdzad sogs dge tshul nyer bzhi rnams bsgrubs /
dol chos rdzod par yar rgyab byang ba sogs mang pos phul ba'i rang byon ring bsrel ska brnyan sogs mang tsam yod pa rnams dol gsung gling phar byung 'dug pa nas spyan snga grags pa 'byung gnas kyi zhun thigs las grub pa'i spyan ras gzigs phyag stong spyan stong gi snang brnyan gyi mthar /
rje btsun grags pa /
sa paN /
byang sems zla rgyal /
jo mo tsha rtsim /
rgyal sras thogs med /
rgyal thang ba /
mkhan chen don yod rgyal mtshan /
mkhan chen grags rgyal ba rnams kyi yungs 'bru lta bu'i ring bsrel gyis bskar zhing /
mi la'i ras gos /
kha che paN chen /
sa paN /
khro lo /
bu ston rnams kyi dbu lo bzhugs pa'i gan+to la /
'phags chen bsod nams ngar gyi tshems ring bsrel can bzhugs pa'i dngul gdung /
de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung sharI ram /
bram ze mchog sred /
sha bo sgang ba /
rje btsun grags pa /
kun mkhyen dol bo pa /
bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan /
rgyal sras thogs med /
dag bcom ba gzhon nu byang chub /
yar klungs pa seng ge rgyal mtshan /
zha lu lo chen chos skyong bzang po rnams kyi ring bsrel /
rje dus gsum mkhyen pa /
'phags chen bsod nams dar /
'phags dbon gsum gyi tshems /
dge slong ma dpal mo'i dbu klad ring bsrel gyi gong bu can /
pha dam pa'i gdung /
karma pa shi'i thugs ring bsrel can dung dkar g.yas 'khyal gyis mchan pa rnams bzhugs pa'i gser zangs kyi rnam rgyal mchod rten /
paN chen nags rin dang 'phags dbon gyi zhun thigs bzhugs pa'i gab tse /
gnyags dbon gyi sku cog gang ma che gra me thub ma /
dus 'khor rgya nag ma tsan+dan dkar po las grub pa dngos gtsang ba /
spyan ras gzigs phyag stong spyan stong kA ma rU ba'i rdo las grub pa /
tsan+dan gor+shiSha las grub pa'i bcu gcig zhal gyi sku /
mkhan po bo d+hi sata'i zhabs rjes la 'od zer 'phros pa'i lhas bskor ba'i bris thang /
'phags dbon gyi nang mchod ka pA la mkha' 'gro sde lnga'i snang brnyan rang byon yod pa /
hor jus kyi rten khebs /
rje btsun grags pa /
sa paN /
'phags pa /
bla ma dam pa /
theg chen chos @# / /
rgyal rnams kyis rim par dbang gdan du bstar ba'i byin rten /
mnyam med jo bo chen po'i chos dung sogs pho brang 'dir bzhugs 'os rnams rtsis blangs shing 'bros rnams phyir prog /
hor zla gnyis pa'i tshes gcig la dpon mo bsod nams chos 'dzom / /
